Parse the priority string during stream initialization\n2. Send PRIORITY_UPDATE frames with the specified urgency and incremental flag\n3. Use the ngtcp2 API to set stream priority (if available)\n\nExample backend integration in `lib/vquic/curl_ngtcp2.c`:\n```c\nif(data->set.h3_stream_priority) {\n  unsigned char urgency = 0;\n  bool incremental = false;\n\n  /* Parse the priority string */\n  sscanf(data->set.h3_stream_priority, \"u=%hhu\", &urgency);\n  if(strchr(data->set.h3_stream_priority, 'i'))\n    incremental = true;\n\n  /* Send PRIORITY_UPDATE frame via ngtcp2 API */\n  /* (implementation depends on ngtcp2/nghttp3 version) */\n}\n```\n\n## Success Criteria\n\n✅ CURLOPT_H3_STREAM_PRIORITY defined in curl.h\n✅ Priority fields added to UserDefined struct\n✅ Option handler in setopt.c\n✅ Entry in easyoptions.c\n✅ CLI option in tool_getparam.c\n✅ Option wiring in tool_operate.c\n✅ Test file created\n✅ Backend integration planned\n\n## Files Modified\n\n1. `include/curl/curl.h` - Option definition\n2. `lib/urldata.h` - Data structure\n3. `lib/setopt.c` - Option handler\n4. `lib/easyoptions.c` - Easy options array\n5. `src/tool_cfgable.h` - CLI configuration struct\n6. `src/tool_getparam.c` - CLI option parsing\n7. `src/tool_operate.c` - CLI option wiring\n8. `tests/unit/unit_h3_priority.c` - Unit tests (new file)\n\n## Testing\n\nRun existing test suite:\n```bash\nmake test\n```\n\nRun unit tests:\n```bash\ntests/unit/unit_h3_priority\n```\n\nIntegration test (requires HTTP/3 server):\n```bash\ncurl --http3 --h3-priority u=3 https://h3.example.com/\n```\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

Conditional on `USE_HTTP3`\n\n3. **lib/setopt.c**\n   - Added case handler for `CURLOPT_H3_STREAM_PRIORITY`\n   - Validates and stores the priority string\n   - Conditional on `USE_HTTP3`\n\n4. **lib/easyoptions.c**\n   - Added entry in `Curl_easyopts` array\n   - Maps option name to CURLOPT value\n\n5. **src/tool_cfgable.h**\n   - Added `h3_stream_priority` field to `OperationConfig` struct\n   - Stores CLI option value\n\n6. **src/tool_getparam.c**\n   - Added `\"0h\"` short option and `\"h3-priority\"` long option\n   - Type: `ARG_STRING`\n\n7. **src/tool_operate.c**\n   - Added code to wire CLI option to CURL option\n   - Calls `my_setopt_str()` with the priority string\n\n8. **tests/unit/unit_h3_priority.c** (NEW)\n   - Parse the priority string during stream setup\n2. Send PRIORITY_UPDATE frames with appropriate urgency and incremental flag\n3. Use ngtcp2/nghttp3 APIs to set stream priority\n\n## Error Handling\n\n- If HTTP/3 is not built in: Returns `CURLE_NOT_BUILT_IN`\n- If priority string is invalid: Returns `CURLE_BAD_FUNCTION_ARGUMENT`\n- If setting fails: Returns appropriate error code from backend\n\n## Backward Compatibility\n\n- No impact on existing code or options\n- Option is only available when HTTP/3 is compiled in\n- Graceful fallback to error when HTTP/3 not available\n\n## Future Enhancements\n\nPotential future improvements:\n1.
